***закупать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закупать.html>закупа́ть</a> (17219)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закупить.html>закупи́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakupítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закупать.html>закупа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakupátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закупить.html>закупи́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to buy, to buy in, to buy up</li>
<li>to lay in a stock <i>(of)</i></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:купать.html>купа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kupátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закупать.html>закупа́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakupátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li>to bathe <i>(till/until)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закупать.html>закупа́ли</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ребенок.html>ребёнка</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:до.html>до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:простуда.html>просту́ды</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakupáli</b> rebjónka do prostúdy</i> ― <span class="e-translation">(they) gave the child a cold by bathing it too long</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закупорить.html>заку́порить</a> (20084)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">ку́порить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kúporitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закупорить.html>заку́порить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakúporitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">заку́поривать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to plug, to cork, to clog</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to block</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to strand</li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закурить.html>закури́ть</a> (2024)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kurítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закурить.html>закури́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakurítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закуривать.html>заку́ривать</a></b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:курить.html>кури́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to start smoking, to light up
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>У</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вы.html>вас</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:найтись.html>найдётся</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:закурить.html>закури́ть</a></b>?</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">U vas ne najdjótsja <b>zakurítʹ</b>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Do you have a spare smoke?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закурить.html>закури́</a></b>/<b><a href = vnd.unilang:закурить.html>закури́те</a></b>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakurí</b>/<b>zakuríte</b>!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">have a cigar!, have a cigarette!</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to become a smoker, to take up smoking</li>
<li>to smoke something through (e.g. make a room full of (cigarette) smoke)</li></ol>

***закусить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закусить.html>закуси́ть</a> (5062)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">куси́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">kusítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закусить.html>закуси́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakusítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закусывать.html>заку́сывать</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bite
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закусить.html>закуси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>гу́бы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakusítʹ</b> gúby</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bite one's lip</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закусить.html>закуси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakusítʹ</b> jazýk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to keep one's mouth shut; hold one's tongue</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закусить.html>закуси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удила.html>удила́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakusítʹ</b> udilá (i)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get/take the bit between one's teeth</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to have a snack, to get a bite, to eat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закусить.html>закуси́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наскоро.html>на́скоро</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakusítʹ</b> náskoro</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to snatch a quick bite</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(eating)</i> to take <i>(with)</i>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_3">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закуска.html>заку́ска</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakúska</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закуска.html>заку́ски</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закуска.html>заку́ски</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закуска.html>заку́сок</a></b>)

<h4><span id=".D0.A1.D0.B8.D0.BD.D0.BE.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.BC.D1.8B"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Синонимы"><a href = vnd.unilang:синоним.html>Сино́нимы</a></span></h4>
<ol><li>частич.: трактирный</li>
</ol>

***закусывать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:закусывать.html>заку́сывать</a> (7097)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закусить.html>закуси́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zakusítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ывать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-yvatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закусывать.html>заку́сывать</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zakúsyvatʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:закусить.html>закуси́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to bite
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закусывать.html>заку́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:губа.html>гу́бы</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakúsyvatʹ</b> gúby</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to bite one's lip</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закусывать.html>заку́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:язык.html>язы́к</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakúsyvatʹ</b> jazýk</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to keep one's mouth shut; hold one's tongue</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закусывать.html>заку́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:удила.html>удила́</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakúsyvatʹ</b> udilá (i)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to get/take the bit between one's teeth</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to have a snack, to get a bite, to eat
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закусывать.html>заку́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:наскоро.html>на́скоро</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakúsyvatʹ</b> náskoro</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to snatch a quick bite</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><i>(eating)</i> to take <i>(with)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закусывать.html>заку́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>ры́бой</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakúsyvatʹ</b> rýboj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to have a bit of fish</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:закусывать.html>заку́сывать</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:водка.html>во́дку</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:рыба.html>ры́бой</a> (<a href = vnd.unilang:колбаса.html>колбасо́й</a>)</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zakúsyvatʹ</b> vódku rýboj (kolbasój)</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to drink vodka with fish (sausage)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***заладить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:заладить.html>зала́дить</a> (21966)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладить.html>ла́дить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">láditʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:заладить.html>зала́дить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">zaláditʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ладить.html>ла́дить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to keep talking <i>(about)</i>, to harp <i>(on/about)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заладить.html>зала́дить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:один.html>одно́</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:тот.html>то</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:же.html>же</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaláditʹ</b> odnó i to že</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to harp on the same tune</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to take <i>(to)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:заладить.html>зала́дил</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ходить.html>ходи́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:кино.html>кино́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">on <b>zaládil</b> xodítʹ v kinó</i> ― <span class="e-translation">he has taken to going to the cinema [to the movies]</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:заладить.html>зала́дили</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:дождь.html>дожди́</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>zaládili</b> doždí</i> ― <span class="e-translation">it began to rain most of the time</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">за-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">za-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:латать.html>лата́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">latátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
